href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-native-interface-xcomponent-h#oh_nativexcomponent_gethistoricalpoints">int32_t OH_NativeXComponent_GetHistoricalPoints(OH_NativeXComponent* component, const void* window, int32_t* size, OH_NativeXComponent_HistoricalPoint** historicalPoints)</a></td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">获取当前XComponent触摸事件的历史点信息。由于部分输入设备上报触点的频率非常高（最高可达每1 ms上报一次），而对输入事件的响应通常是为了使UI界面发生变化以响应用户操作，如果将触摸事件按照上报触点的频率如此高频率上报给应用，大多会造成冗余，因此触摸事件在一帧内只会上报一次给应用。在当前帧内上报的触点均作为历史点保存，如果应用需要直接处理这些数据，可调用该接口获取历史点信息。</td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-native-interface-xcomponent-h#oh_nativexcomponent_getmouseevent">int32_t OH_NativeXComponent_GetMouseEvent(OH_NativeXComponent* component, const void* window, OH_NativeXComponent_MouseEvent* mouseEvent)</a></td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">获取ArkUI XComponent调度的鼠标事件。</td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-native-interface-xcomponent-h#oh_nativexcomponent_registercallback">int32_t OH_NativeXComponent_RegisterCallback(OH_NativeXComponent* component, class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.13.6.1.3.1.1" width="50%">枚举项</th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.13.6.1.3.1.2" width="50%">描述</th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">OH_NATIVEXCOMPONENT_MOUSE_NONE = 0</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">无效鼠标事件。</td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">OH_NATIVEXCOMPONENT_MOUSE_PRESS = 1</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">鼠标按键按下时触发鼠标事件。</td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">OH_NATIVEXCOMPONENT_MOUSE_RELEASE = 2</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">鼠标按键松开时触发鼠标事件。</td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">OH_NATIVEXCOMPONENT_MOUSE_MOVE = 3</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">鼠标在屏幕上移动时触发鼠标事件。</td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">OH_NATIVEXCOMPONENT_MOUSE_CANCEL = 4</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>鼠标按键被取消时触发鼠标事件。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 18 </p> <p> <strong>说明：</strong> OH_NATIVEXCOMPONENT_MOUSE_CANCEL表示鼠标事件被取消，通常在以下场景被触发：</p> <p>1.组件失去焦点：当前持有焦点的XComponent因系统事件（如弹窗打断、应用切换）失去焦点时，会触发该动作。</p> <p> 2.事件中断：鼠标操作过程中发生更高优先级事件（如系统级手势或强制回收事件流），导致当前鼠标操作被强制终止。</p> <p>3.异常状态退出：如组件销毁、渲染环境异常等场景下，未完成的鼠标事件会被标记为取消。</p> </td> </tr> class="hljs-params">(OH_NativeXComponent* component, <span class="hljs-type">char</span>* id, <span class="hljs-type">uint64_t</span>* size)</span></span></li></ol></pre></div></div> <p><strong>描述：</strong></p> <p>获取ArkUI XComponent的id。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 8</p> <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.17.7.1.3.1.1" width="50%">参数项</th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.17.7.1.3.1.2" width="50%">描述</th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/vexcomponent-native-xcomponent-oh-nativexcomponent">OH_NativeXComponent</a>* href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/vexcomponent-native-xcomponent-oh-nativexcomponent">OH_NativeXComponent</a>实例的指针。</td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">char* id</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">表示用于保存此<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/vexcomponent-native-xcomponent-oh-nativexcomponent">OH_NativeXComponent</a>实例的ID的字符缓冲区。请注意，空终止符将附加到字符缓冲区，因此字符缓冲区的大小应至少比真实id长度大一个单位。建议字符缓冲区的大小为[<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-native-interface-xcomponent-h#变量">OH_XCOMPONENT_ID_LEN_MAX</a> + 1]。</td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">uint64_t* size</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">表示指向id长度的指针，用于接收id的长度信息。</td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p><strong>返回：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.17.9.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.17.9.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">int32_t</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>返回执行的状态代码。</p> <p><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-native-interface-xcomponent-h#anonymous">OH_NATIVEXCOMPONENT_RESULT_SUCCESS</a> - 执行成功。</p> <p><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-native-interface-xcomponent-h#anonymous">OH_NATIVEXCOMPONENT_RESULT_BAD_PARAMETER</a> - 传入参数异常。</p> </td> </tr> XComponent持有的Surface的大小。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 8</p> <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/vexcomponent-native-xcomponent-oh-nativexcomponent">OH_NativeXComponent</a>* component</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">表示指向<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/vexcomponent-native-xcomponent-oh-nativexcomponent">OH_NativeXComponent</a>实例的指针。</td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" <p>获取当前XComponent触摸事件的历史点信息。由于部分输入设备上报触点的频率非常高（最高可达每1 ms上报一次），而对输入事件的响应通常是为了使UI界面发生变化以响应用户操作，如果将触摸事件按照上报触点的频率如此高频率上报给应用，大多会造成冗余，因此触摸事件在一帧内只会上报一次给应用。在当前帧内上报的触点均作为历史点保存，如果应用需要直接处理这些数据，可调用该接口获取历史点信息。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 10</p> <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.28.7.1.3.1.1" width="50%">参数项</th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.28.7.1.3.1.2" width="50%">描述</th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/vexcomponent-native-xcomponent-oh-nativexcomponent">OH_NativeXComponent</a>* component</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">表示指向<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/vexcomponent-native-xcomponent-oh-nativexcomponent">OH_NativeXComponent</a>实例的指针。</td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">const void* window</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">表示NativeWindow句柄。</td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">int32_t* size</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">表示当前历史接触点数组的长度。</td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ive-xcomponent-oh-nativexcomponent-historicalpoint">OH_NativeXComponent_HistoricalPoint</a>** historicalPoints</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">表示指向当前历史接触点数组的指针。</td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p><strong>返回：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.28.9.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.28.9.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">int32_t</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>返回执行的状态代码。</p> <p><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-native-interface-xcomponent-h#anonymous">OH_NATIVEXCOMPONENT_RESULT_BAD_PARAMETER</a> - 传入参数异常。</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> </div>  <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 926px;"><h3 id="oh_nativexcomponent_getmouseevent" width="50%"><p>表示XComponent组件是否需要自动初始化Surface。如果autoInitialize值是true，OnSurfaceCreated回调会在挂树时被触发，OnSurfaceDestroyed回调会在下树时被触发。false表示组件不需要自动初始化Surface。</p> <p>autoInitialize默认值是true。</p> </td> </tr>
